# This is data generated from a modified Doob-Gillespie aglorithm for N_group=50 contact groups each containing G_size=20 individuals 
# An SIR model is assumed.
# Simulation is performed from between time t=-5 and t = 5 until t=100.
# beta=0.015, gamma=0.1, k=5 were used for the epidemiological parameters.
# a_g=0.4, a_f=0.3, a_r=-0.4, delta_g=0.4, delta_f=0.1, delta_r=-0.3 where used for the SNP parameters with A allele frequency p=0.3.
# b_g0=0.2, b_f0=0.3, b_r0=-0.2 were used for a single fixed effect (individuals randomly allocated into two classifications, e.g. sex).
# Sigma_gg=0.5, Sigma_gf=0.15, Sigma_gr=-0.2, Sigma_ff=0.5, Sigma_fr=-0.1, Sigma_rr=0.5 was used for the residual covariance matrix.
# sigma_G=0.25 was used for the standard deviation in the group effect.

# The columns are as follows:
# "ID" relates to individual IDs.
# "Time" relates to the time at which the disease status measurement is made
# "Status" relates to the disease status measurement (S, I or R)
# "Group" gives the contact group an individual belongs to
# "SNP" gives the genotype of an an individual at the SNP under investigation
# "Sex" where 0/1 relates to male/female.
# "Type" give the initial infection status of individuals ("Seeder" means infected at t=0 and "Contact" means susceptible).

ID	Time	Status	Group	SNP	Sex	Type
